10/05/2016 09:29:41.417 AM Sending - Multi protocol tag op, TMR_SR_OPCODE_MULTI_PROTOCOL_TAG_OP
    FF  10  2F  00  00  01  22  00  00  05  07  22  10  00  1B  03 E8  01  FF  DD  2B
	
	00 00 = timeout (zero for continuous reading
	01 = "TM option 1 for continuous reading" 

/* Timeout should be zero for true continuous reading */
SETU16(msg, i, 0);
SETU8(msg, i, (uint8_t)0x1);//TM Option 1, for continuous reading

	(i = 6) 22 = subcommand opcode, is TMR_SR_OPCODE_READ_TAG_ID_MULTIPLE
	
	(7, 8) 00 00 = I think: don't stop after NTags, 'search flags'
	
	(9) 05 = "sub protocol ID" - protocol ID to search for? line 3606
	
	(10) 07 = "PLEN" = protocol length? 
	
	(Add additional bytes via sub function TMR_SR_msgSetupReadTagMultipleWithMetadata)
	
	22 = opcode TMR_SR_OPCODE_READ_TAG_ID_MULTIPLE
	10 = option byte
	00 =
